			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = ABY_operations_4_1
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = ABY_first_focus_tt_42
				set_country_flag = ABY_operations_4_2
				clr_country_flag = ABY_operations_4_1
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					NOT = {
						OR = {
							has_country_flag = ABY_operations_4_1
							has_country_flag = ABY_operations_4_2
							has_country_flag = ABY_operations_4_3
						}
					}
				}
				custom_effect_tooltip = ABY_first_focus_tt_41
				set_country_flag = ABY_operations_4_1
			}
		}
	}

ABY_descision_category_fortress = {
	ABY_descision_tepliche_fortress_1 = {
		days_remove = 25
		priority = 1
		fire_only_once = yes
		cost = 25
		visible = {
			tag = ABY
			has_completed_focus = ABY_focus_border_fortress
		}
		modifier = {
			civilian_factory_use = 3
		}
        allowed = {
            tag = ABY
        }
		available = {
			controls_state = 985
		}
		remove_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { controls_state = 985 }
				985 = {
					set_building_level = {
						type = bunker
						level = 4
						province = {
							limit_to_border = yes
							level < 4
						}
					}
				}
			}
			set_country_flag = ABY_flag_tepliche_fortress_1
		}
	}

ABY_descision_category_german_terrorist = {
	ABY_descision_debug_100 = {
		priority = 1
		
		visible = {
			tag = ABY
			has_country_flag = ABY_flag_german_terrorist
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = ABY_flag_german_finish
			}
			is_debug = yes
		}
		
        allowed = {
            tag = ABY
        }

		complete_effect = {
			
			add_to_variable = {
   		        var = ABY_terrorist_var
   		        value = 100
   		        tooltip = ABY_german_plus_100_tt
   		    }
		}
	}
	ABY_descision_german_agent = {
		days_remove = 30
		priority = 1
		fire_only_once = yes
		cost = 25
		visible = {
			tag = ABY
			has_country_flag = ABY_flag_german_terrorist
			NOT = {
				has_country_flag = ABY_flag_german_finish
			}
		}
		available = {
			NOT = {
				check_variable = {
            	    var = ABY_terrorist_var

			FROM = {
				exists = yes

	ABY_descision_school_millenium = {
        priority = 1

        allowed = {
            tag = ABY
        }

		visible = {
			tag = ABY
			has_country_flag = ABY_flag_only_school
		}

        available = {
			any_state = {
				is_core_of = MIL
				is_controlled_by = ABY
			}
        }

		fire_only_once = yes

		cost = 150

		days_remove = 30

        remove_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = ABY_idea_only_school_1
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = ABY_idea_only_school_1
					add_idea = ABY_idea_only_school_2
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_idea = ABY_idea_only_school_2
				}
				swap_ideas = {
					remove_idea = ABY_idea_only_school_2
					add_idea = ABY_idea_only_school_3
				}
			}
        }
	}
